<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h1 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0430769s;" class="preFade fadeIn">PRIVACY POLICY</h1>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer sized vsize-1" data-block-type="21" id="block-36f0fc6188abbbbf6287"><div class="sqs-block-content">&nbsp;</div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-45b1431f30442b13e432"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0461538s;" class="preFade fadeIn">Thank you for your interest in The Twilight Zone VR, a virtual reality game (the “Game”).  The Twilight Zone VR  is offered by Fun Train Media, LLC. (“FTM”) a wholly owned subsidiary of Fun Train Inc. (Fun Train)</h2>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block horizontalrule-block sqs-block-horizontalrule" data-block-type="47" id="block-cb1d8fee04109b03e204"><div class="sqs-block-content"><hr></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-9ec502d4dc064637df3e"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="text-align: center; white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0492308s;" class="preFade">PRIVACY POLICY</h3><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0523077s;"><strong>Fun Train Inc. Privacy Policy Last Updated: May 13, 2022</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0553846s;">Your privacy is very important to us. Accordingly, we have developed this Policy in order for you to understand how we collect, use, communicate and disclose and make use of personal information. The following outlines our privacy policy.&nbsp; If you have any questions about our privacy policy, please contact <a href="mailto:legal@funtrainvr.com"><span style="text-decoration:underline">legal@funtrainvr.com</span></a> via email or at the address listed in section XIV</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0584615s;">Fun Train Inc. (“Fun Train,” “we,” “us,” and “our”) provides virtual reality (“VR”) gaming experiences through our subsidiaries on the Meta, Steam, PlayStation, Nintendo, Humble and other platforms through games such as The Twilight Zone VR and others. Our subsidiaries include Fun Train Media LLC and others.  This Privacy Policy is designed to help you understand how we collect, use, and share your personal information and to help you understand and exercise your privacy rights. Fun Train is the data controller for the personal information we process. For information on how to contact us, please refer to Section XIV below.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0615385s;">1. SCOPE</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0646154s;">2. PERSONAL INFORMATION WE COLLECT</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0676923s;">3. HOW WE USE YOUR INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0707692s;">4. WHAT IS OUR LEGAL BASIS FOR PROCESSING YOUR INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0738462s;">5. HOW WE SHARE YOUR INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0769231s;">6. YOUR PRIVACY CHOICES AND RIGHTS</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.08s;">7. SECURITY OF YOUR INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0830769s;">8. INTERNATIONAL DATA TRANSFERS</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0861538s;">9. RETENTION OF PERSONAL INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0892308s;">10. SUPPLEMENTAL NOTICE FOR CALIFORNIA RESIDENTS</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0923077s;">11. SUPPLEMENTAL NOTICE FOR NEVADA RESIDENTS</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0953846s;">12. CHILDREN’S INFORMATION</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.0984615s;">13. OTHER PROVISIONS</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.101538s;">13. CONTACT US</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.104615s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">I. SCOPE</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.107692s;">This Privacy Policy applies to personal information processed by us, including on our websites, mobile applications, games, and other online or offline offerings. To make this Privacy Policy easier to read, our websites, mobile applications, games, and other offerings are collectively called “Services”.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.110769s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">II. PERSONAL INFORMATION WE COLLECT</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.113846s;">The categories of personal information we collect depend on how you interact with us, our Services, and the requirements of applicable law. We collect information that you provide to us on our websites and through our mobile applications and games, information we obtain automatically when you use our Services, and information from other sources such as third-party services, organizations and platforms, as described below.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.116923s;">A. Information You Provide to Us Directly</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.12s;">We may collect the following personal information that you provide to us.</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.123077s;">Account Creation. We may collect information from Oculus, Steam or other platforms when you create an account to play our games via such platforms, such as your profile picture, display name, Game Platform User ID, or other information that you have made available via your privacy settings on such platforms.</p></li></ul><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.126154s;">Beta User Information. If you sign up to join a Beta on our Services, we will collect your email address, first name, age, gender, type/model of VR headset, platform type, platform username and Discord username. We will also collect additional information you provide, including via surveys, such as hours playing the games, comfort and estimated motion sickness levels while playing the game and a net promoter score and we will add your email to our mailing list for beta testers. For more information about how to unsubscribe from our email list, please see Section III.C below.</p></li></ul><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.129231s;">Purchases. We may collect aggregate information from Oculus or Steam (e.g., what has been purchased and refund metrics). Any payments made for our Services are processed through Oculus or Steam. We do not collect or store any payment card information for purchases on our Services.</p></li></ul><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.132308s;">Your Communications with Us. We may collect personal information, such as your name and email address, when you complete the “Contact Us” form on our main website or register for our mailing list, User IDs and headset used, details of your request and any attachments you provide when you request customer or technical support and other information you may provide when you apply for a job or otherwise communicate with us.</p></li></ul><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.135385s;">Interactive Features. We and others who use our Services may have access to personal information that you submit or make available through our interactive features (e.g., the games themselves, forums, blogs, and social media pages). Any information you provide on these features will be considered “public”, unless otherwise required by applicable law, and is not subject to the privacy protections referenced herein. Please exercise caution before revealing personal information to strangers via our Services. For more information about third party websites, please see Section XIII below.</p></li></ul><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.138462s;">Sweepstakes or Contests. We may collect personal information you provide for any sweepstakes or contests that we offer. In some jurisdictions, we are required to publicly share information of sweepstakes and contest winners.</p></li></ul><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.141538s;">Business Development and Strategic Partnerships. We may collect personal information from individuals and third parties to assess and pursue potential business opportunities.</p></li></ul><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.144615s;">Job Applications. We may post job openings and opportunities on our Services. If you reply to one of these postings by submitting your application, CV and/or cover letter to us, we will collect and use your information to assess your qualifications.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.147692s;">B. Information Collected Automatically</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.150769s;">We may collect personal information automatically when you use our Services:</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.153846s;">Automatic Data Collection. We may collect certain information automatically when you use our Services, such as your Internet protocol (IP) address, user settings, cookie identifiers and platform identifiers , in game analytics, player event data, information on bugs and crashes browser or device information, general location information (including approximate location derived from IP address), and hardware information such as your GPU (type and clock speed), CPU (type and clock speed), system memory, OS locale, and Internet service provider. We may also automatically collect information regarding your use of our Services, such as pages that you visit before, during and after using our Services, information about the links you click, the types of content you interact with, the frequency and duration of your activities, and other information about how you use our Services.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.156923s;">Cookies, Pixel Tags/Web Beacons, and Other Technologies. We, as well as third parties that provide content, advertising, or other functionality on our Services, may use cookies, pixel tags, local storage, and other technologies (“Technologies”) to automatically collect information through your use of our Services. For more information see our Cookies Policy. You can change your preferences here.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.16s;">C. transition-delay: 0.461538s;">IDENTIFIERS: Audio, electronic, visual, or similar information.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.486154s;">“Sales” of Personal Information under the CCPA</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.489231s;">For purposes of the CCPA, Fun Train does not “sell” personal information, nor do we have actual knowledge of any “sale” of personal information of minors under 16 years of age.</p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.492308s;"></p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.495385s;">Additional Privacy Rights for California Residents</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.498462s;">If you are a California resident, subject to certain exceptions and applicable law, you may have certain rights in relation to information we process about you</p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.501538s;">Right to Know. In relation to your right to access described above, you may request that we disclose to you the categories and specific pieces of personal information that we have collected about you in the preceding 12 months, the categories of sources from which your personal information is collected, the business or commercial purpose for collecting your personal information, the categories of personal information that we disclosed for a business purpose in the preceding 12 months, the categories of third parties with whom we have shared your personal information, and the business or commercial purpose for each disclosure.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.504615s;">Right to Delete. In relation to your right to delete as described above, you may request that we delete any personal information that we have collected from you.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.507692s;">Non-Discrimination. You have the right not to receive discriminatory treatment by us for the exercise of their rights conferred by the CCPA.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.510769s;">Authorized Agent. Only you, or someone legally authorized to act on your behalf, may make a verifiable consumer request related to your personal information. You may also make a verifiable consumer request on behalf of your minor child. To designate an authorized agent, please contact us as set forth in Section XIV below.</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.513846s;">Verification. To protect your privacy, we will take the following steps to verify your identity before fulfilling your request. When you make a request, we will ask you to provide sufficient information that allows us to reasonably verify you are the person about whom we collected personal information or an authorized representative, which may include your name, email address, or Game Platform User ID.</p></li></ul></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.516923s;">If you are a California resident and would like to exercise any of your rights under the CCPA, please contact us as set forth in Section XIV below. We will process such requests in accordance with applicable laws.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.52s;">Accessibility. This Privacy Policy uses industry-standard technologies and was developed in line with the World Wide Web Consortium’s Web Content Accessibility Guidelines, version 2.1. If you wish to print this policy, please do so from your web browser or by saving the page as a PDF.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.523077s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">XI. SUPPLEMENTAL NOTICE FOR NEVADA RESIDENTS</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.526154s;">If you are a resident of Nevada, you have the right to opt-out of the sale of certain Personal Information to third parties who intend to license or sell that Personal Information. Please note that we do not currently sell your Personal Information as sales are defined in Nevada Revised Statutes Chapter 603A. If you have any questions, please contact us as set forth in Section XIV below.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.529231s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">XII. CHILDREN’S INFORMATION</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.532308s;">The Services are not directed to children under 13 (or other age as required by local law), and we do not knowingly collect personal information from children.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.535385s;">If you are a parent or guardian and wish to review information collected from your child, or have that information modified or deleted, you may contact us as described in Section XIV below. If we become aware that a child has provided us with personal information in violation of applicable law, we will delete any personal information we have collected, unless we have a legal obligation to keep it, and terminate the child’s account and/or revert them to the underage experience, as applicable.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.538462s;"><span style="text-decoration:underline">XIII. OTHER PROVISIONS</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.541538s;">Third-Party Websites/Applications. The Services may contain links to other websites/applications and other websites/applications may reference or link to our Services. These third-party services are not controlled by us. We encourage our users to read the privacy policies of each website and application with which they interact. We do not endorse, screen or approve, and are not responsible for, the privacy practices or content of such other websites or applications. Providing personal information to third-party websites or applications is at your own risk.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.544615s;">Supervisory Authority. You may have the right to lodge a complaint with your local supervisory authority if you believe our processing of your personal information violates applicable law including in the EU and UK.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.9s; transition-delay: 0.547692s;">Changes to our Privacy Policy.             sectionBackground.style.top = '';
